  é˜¶æ®µ2: é›†æˆéªé¾™NPUåŠ é€Ÿ (æ ¸å¿ƒå·¥ä½œ)

  å‚è€ƒ èµ„æ–™å‚è€ƒ/command.txt ä¸­çš„ç¯å¢ƒ:

  åˆ›å»º deploy_qwen2.py:
  # deploy_qwen2.py - éƒ¨ç½²Qwen2åˆ°éªé¾™NPU
  import qai_appbuilder as qai
  from pathlib import Path

  def deploy_qwen2_npu():
      """éƒ¨ç½²Qwen2-1.5Båˆ°éªé¾™NPU"""

      print("=" * 50)
      print("Antinet - éƒ¨ç½²Qwen2åˆ°éªé¾™NPU")
      print("=" * 50)

      # é…ç½®
      config = {
          "model_name": "qwen2-1.5b",
          "backend": "QNN",
          "device": "NPU",
          "precision": "INT8",  # é‡åŒ–ä»¥æå‡æ€§èƒ½
          "cache_dir": "./models"
      }

      print(f"\n[1/4] ä¸‹è½½Qwen2-1.5Bæ¨¡å‹...")
      # ä»Hugging Faceæˆ–æœ¬åœ°è·¯å¾„åŠ è½½
      model_path = qai.hub.download_model(config["model_name"])

      print(f"\n[2/4] è½¬æ¢æ¨¡å‹ä¸ºQNNæ ¼å¼...")
      # è½¬æ¢ä¸ºONNXå†è½¬QNN
      onnx_model = qai.convert_to_onnx(model_path)
      qnn_model = qai.convert_to_qnn(onnx_model,
                                       device="NPU",
                                       precision="INT8")

      print(f"\n[3/4] ç¼–è¯‘æ¨¡å‹åˆ°NPU...")
      compiled_model = qai.compile_for_npu(qnn_model)

      print(f"\n[4/4] ä¿å­˜ç¼–è¯‘åçš„æ¨¡å‹...")
      output_path = Path("./models/qwen2-1.5b-npu.bin")
      qai.save_model(compiled_model, output_path)

      print(f"\nâœ“ æ¨¡å‹éƒ¨ç½²å®Œæˆ!")
      print(f"  è·¯å¾„: {output_path}")
      print(f"  åç«¯: {config['backend']}")
      print(f"  è®¾å¤‡: {config['device']}")

      # æ€§èƒ½æµ‹è¯•
      print(f"\n[æ€§èƒ½æµ‹è¯•] æµ‹è¯•NPUæ¨ç†å»¶è¿Ÿ...")
      test_input = "åˆ†æä¸Šä¸ªæœˆçš„é”€å”®æ•°æ®"
      latency = qai.benchmark_inference(compiled_model, test_input)
      print(f"  å¹³å‡å»¶è¿Ÿ: {latency:.2f}ms")

      return compiled_model

  if __name__ == "__main__":
      deploy_qwen2_npu()

  2.2 é›†æˆåˆ°å‰ç«¯åº”ç”¨

  åˆ›å»ºåç«¯APIæœåŠ¡ (backend/server.py):
  # backend/server.py - æ•°æ®åˆ†æåç«¯æœåŠ¡
  from fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException
  from pydantic import BaseSettings, BaseModel
  import qai_appbuilder as qai
  import json

  app = FastAPI(title="Antinetæ•°æ®åˆ†æAPI")

  # åŠ è½½NPUæ¨¡å‹
  print("åŠ è½½Qwen2-NPUæ¨¡å‹...")
  model = qai.load_model("./models/qwen2-1.5b-npu.bin", device="NPU")
  print("âœ“ æ¨¡å‹åŠ è½½å®Œæˆ")

  class QueryRequest(BaseModel):
      query: str  # è‡ªç„¶è¯­è¨€æŸ¥è¯¢
      data_source: str  # æ•°æ®æº (local/feishu/dingtalk)
      context: dict = {}  # é¢å¤–ä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡

  class AnalysisResult(BaseModel):
      facts: list[str]  # äº‹å®å¡ç‰‡
      explanations: list[str]  # è§£é‡Šå¡ç‰‡
      risks: list[str]  # é£é™©å¡ç‰‡
      actions: list[str]  # è¡ŒåŠ¨å¡ç‰‡
      visualizations: list[dict]  # å¯è§†åŒ–é…ç½®

  @app.post("/api/analyze", response_model=AnalysisResult)
  async def analyze_data(request: QueryRequest):
      """è‡ªç„¶è¯­è¨€é©±åŠ¨çš„æ•°æ®åˆ†æ"""

      try:
          # 1. ä½¿ç”¨NPUæ¨¡å‹ç†è§£æŸ¥è¯¢æ„å›¾
          print(f"[NPUæ¨ç†] åˆ†ææŸ¥è¯¢: {request.query}")
          intent = model.infer(
              prompt=f"åˆ†æä»¥ä¸‹æ•°æ®æŸ¥è¯¢è¯·æ±‚ï¼Œæå–å…³é”®ä¿¡æ¯ï¼š{request.query}",
              max_tokens=512
          )

          # 2. æ‰§è¡Œæ•°æ®æŸ¥è¯¢ (æœ¬åœ°å¤„ç†)
          # è¿™é‡Œåº”è¯¥è¿æ¥æœ¬åœ°æ•°æ®åº“æˆ–é€šè¿‡APIè·å–æ•°æ®
          data = fetch_data_locally(request.data_source, intent)

          # 3. ä½¿ç”¨NPUæ¨¡å‹ç”Ÿæˆå››è‰²å¡ç‰‡åˆ†æ
          analysis_prompt = f"""
          åŸºäºä»¥ä¸‹æ•°æ®ï¼Œç”Ÿæˆå››è‰²å¡ç‰‡åˆ†æï¼š
          æ•°æ®: {json.dumps(data)}
          æŸ¥è¯¢: {request.query}

          è¯·åˆ†åˆ«ç”Ÿæˆï¼š
          1. äº‹å®(Facts): å®¢è§‚æ•°æ®ç»“æœ
          2. è§£é‡Š(Explanations): æ•°æ®èƒŒåçš„åŸå› 
          3. é£é™©(Risks): æ½œåœ¨é—®é¢˜å’Œé£é™©ç‚¹
          4. è¡ŒåŠ¨(Actions): å…·ä½“è¡ŒåŠ¨å»ºè®®

          ä»¥JSONæ ¼å¼è¿”å›ã€‚
          """

          analysis = model.infer(prompt=analysis_prompt, max_tokens=1024)
          result = json.loads(analysis)

          # 4. ç”Ÿæˆå¯è§†åŒ–é…ç½®
          visualizations = generate_visualizations(data, intent)

          return AnalysisResult(
              facts=result.get("facts", []),
              explanations=result.get("explanations", []),
              risks=result.get("risks", []),
              actions=result.get("actions", []),
              visualizations=visualizations
          )

      except Exception as e:
          raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

  def fetch_data_locally(source: str, intent: dict) -> dict:
      """æœ¬åœ°åŒ–æ•°æ®è·å– - æ•°æ®ä¸å‡ºåŸŸ"""
      # å®ç°æœ¬åœ°æ•°æ®åº“æŸ¥è¯¢æˆ–APIè°ƒç”¨
      # å…³é”®: åŸå§‹æ•°æ®ä¸å‘é€åˆ°äº‘ç«¯
      return {"mock": "data"}

  def generate_visualizations(data: dict, intent: dict) -> list[dict]:
      """ç”Ÿæˆå¯è§†åŒ–é…ç½®"""
      return [
          {"type": "line", "data": data, "config": {}}
      ]

  @app.get("/api/health")
  async def health_check():
      """å¥åº·æ£€æŸ¥"""
      return {
          "status": "healthy",
          "model": "qwen2-1.5b",
          "device": "NPU",
          "service": "Antinetæ•°æ®åˆ†æAPI"
      }

  if __name__ == "__main__":
      import uvicorn
      uvicorn.run(app, host="0.0.0.0", port=8000)

  2.3 å‰ç«¯é›†æˆè‡ªç„¶è¯­è¨€æŸ¥è¯¢

  ä¿®æ”¹å‰ç«¯ä»£ç  (src/components/DataAnalysisPanel.tsx):
  // src/components/DataAnalysisPanel.tsx
  import React, { useState } from 'react';
  import { Search, Loader, TrendingUp } from 'lucide-react';
  import { toast } from 'sonner';

  interface AnalysisResult {
    facts: string[];
    explanations: string[];
    risks: string[];
    actions: string[];
    visualizations: any[];
  }

  export const DataAnalysisPanel: React.FC = () => {
    const [query, setQuery] = useState('');
    const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
    const [result, setResult] = useState<AnalysisResult | null>(null);

    const handleAnalyze = async () => {
      if (!query.trim()) return;

      setLoading(true);
      try {
        const response = await fetch('http://localhost:8000/api/analyze', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            query: query,
            data_source: 'local',
            context: {}
          })
        });

        if (!response.ok) throw new Error('åˆ†æå¤±è´¥');

        const data = await response.json();
        setResult(data);

        // è‡ªåŠ¨åˆ›å»ºå››è‰²å¡ç‰‡
        createFourColorCards(data);

        toast('åˆ†æå®Œæˆï¼å››è‰²å¡ç‰‡å·²è‡ªåŠ¨ç”Ÿæˆ', {
          className: 'bg-green-50 text-green-800'
        });

      } catch (error) {
        toast('åˆ†æå¤±è´¥ï¼Œè¯·æ£€æŸ¥åç«¯æœåŠ¡', {
          className: 'bg-red-50 text-red-800'
        });
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    };

    const createFourColorCards = (analysis: AnalysisResult) => {
      // åˆ›å»ºè“è‰²å¡ç‰‡(äº‹å®)
      analysis.facts.forEach(fact => {
        createCard({ title: 'æ•°æ®äº‹å®', content: fact, color: 'blue' });
      });

      // åˆ›å»ºç»¿è‰²å¡ç‰‡(è§£é‡Š)
      analysis.explanations.forEach(exp => {
        createCard({ title: 'åŸå› è§£é‡Š', content: exp, color: 'green' });
      });

      // åˆ›å»ºé»„è‰²å¡ç‰‡(é£é™©)
      analysis.risks.forEach(risk => {
        createCard({ title: 'é£é™©é¢„è­¦', content: risk, color: 'yellow' });
      });

      // åˆ›å»ºçº¢è‰²å¡ç‰‡(è¡ŒåŠ¨)
      analysis.actions.forEach(action => {
        createCard({ title: 'è¡ŒåŠ¨å»ºè®®', content: action, color: 'red' });
      });
    };

    return (
      <div className="bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 rounded-xl p-6">
        <h2 className="text-xl font-bold mb-4 flex items-center">
          <TrendingUp className="mr-2" size={20} />
          æ™ºèƒ½æ•°æ®åˆ†æ
        </h2>

        <div className="flex gap-3 mb-6">
          <div className="relative flex-1">
            <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400" size={18} />
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="ä¾‹å¦‚: ä¸Šä¸ªæœˆé”€å”®é¢è¶‹åŠ¿æ˜¯ä»€ä¹ˆï¼Ÿ"
              value={query}
              onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
              onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleAnalyze()}
              className="w-full pl-10 pr-4 py-3 border rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            />
          </div>
          <button
            onClick={handleAnalyze}
            disabled={loading}
            className="px-6 py-3 bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-700 text-white rounded-lg flex items-center gap-2 disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {loading ? <Loader className="animate-spin" size={16} /> : <Search size={16} />}
            åˆ†æ
          </button>
        </div>

        {result && (
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            {/* å››è‰²å¡ç‰‡å±•ç¤º */}
            <CardPreview title="äº‹å®" items={result.facts} color="blue" />
            <CardPreview title="è§£é‡Š" items={result.explanations} color="green" />
            <CardPreview title="é£é™©" items={result.risks} color="yellow" />
            <CardPreview title="è¡ŒåŠ¨" items={result.actions} color="red" />
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    );
  };

  def benchmark_npu_acceleration():
